<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude responds well to clear, explicit instructions. Being specific about your desired output can help enhance results. If you want &quot;above and beyond&quot; behavior, explicitly request it rather than relying on the model to infer this from vague prompts.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Think of Claude as a brilliant but new employee who lacks context on your norms and workflows. The more precisely you explain what you want, the better the result.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Golden rule:</strong> Show your prompt to a colleague with minimal context on the task and ask them to follow it. If they&#x27;d be confused, Claude will be too.</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Be specific about the desired output format and constraints.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Provide instructions as sequential steps using numbered lists or bullet points when the order or completeness of steps matters.</li>¶
</ul>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Providing context or motivation behind your instructions, such as explaining to Claude why such behavior is important, can help Claude better understand your goals and deliver more targeted responses.</p>¶
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_11eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_1eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example: Formatting preferences</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_11eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example:-formatting-preferences" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude is smart enough to generalize from the explanation.</p>¶
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="use-examples-effectively"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.08em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Use examples effectively</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h3>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Examples are one of the most reliable ways to steer Claude&#x27;s output format, tone, and structure. A few well-crafted examples (known as few-shot or multishot prompting) can dramatically improve accuracy and consistency.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">When adding examples, make them:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Relevant:</strong> Mirror your actual use case closely.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Diverse:</strong> Cover edge cases and vary enough that Claude doesn&#x27;t pick up unintended patterns.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Structured:</strong> Wrap examples in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;example&gt;</code> tags (multiple examples in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;examples&gt;</code> tags) so Claude can distinguish them from instructions.</li>¶
</ul>¶
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg px-4 py-3 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-border-200 bg-bg-200 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-text-000"><div style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 17C12.7761 17 13 17.2239 13 17.5C13 17.7761 12.7761 18 12.5 18H7.5C7.22386 18 7 17.7761 7 17.5C7 17.2239 7.22386 17 7.5 17H12.5ZM10 2C13.3137 2 16 4.68629 16 8C16 9.73776 15.2608 11.3033 14.0811 12.3984L13.8389 12.6113C13.3268 13.0382 13 13.5753 13 14.124V15.5C13 15.7761 12.7761 16 12.5 16H7.5C7.22386 16 7 15.7761 7 15.5V14.124C6.99998 13.6438 6.7495 13.1727 6.34375 12.7764L6.16113 12.6113C4.84147 11.5115 4 9.85368 4 8C4 4.68629 6.68629 2 10 2ZM10 3C7.23858 3 5 5.23858 5 8C5 9.5443 5.69948 10.9248 6.80078 11.8428L7.03711 12.0557C7.57356 12.5787 7.99998 13.2899 8 14.124V15H9.5V11.207L7.14648 8.85352L7.08203 8.77539C6.95387 8.58131 6.97562 8.31735 7.14648 8.14648C7.31735 7.97562 7.58131 7.95387 7.77539 8.08203L7.85352 8.14648L10 10.293L12.1465 8.14648L12.2246 8.08203C12.4187 7.95387 12.6827 7.97562 12.8535 8.14648C13.0244 8.31735 13.0461 8.58131 12.918 8.77539L12.8535 8.85352L10.5 11.207V15H12V14.124C12 13.1706 12.5575 12.3776 13.1992 11.8428L13.4004 11.665C14.3848 10.7513 15 9.44786 15 8C15 5.23858 12.7614 3 10 3Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed [&amp;&gt;*:last-child]:mb-0 text-text-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-text-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-text-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-text-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-text-000/10">Include 3–5 examples for best results. You can also ask Claude to evaluate your examples for relevance and diversity, or to generate additional ones based on your initial set.</div></div>¶
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="structure-prompts-with-xml-tags"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.08em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Structure prompts with XML tags</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h3>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">XML tags help Claude parse complex prompts unambiguously, especially when your prompt mixes instructions, context, examples, and variable inputs. Wrapping each type of content in its own tag — e.g. <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;instructions&gt;</code>, <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;context&gt;</code>, <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;input&gt;</code> — reduces misinterpretation.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Best practices:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Use consistent, descriptive tag names across your prompts.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Nest tags when content has a natural hierarchy (documents inside <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;documents&gt;</code>, each inside <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;document index=&quot;n&quot;&gt;</code>).</li>¶
</ul>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Setting a role in the system prompt focuses Claude&#x27;s behavior and tone for your use case. Even a single sentence makes a difference:</p>¶
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><div class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="--shiki-light:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6;--shiki-light-bg:transparent;--shiki-dark-bg:transparent" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> anthropic</span></span>¶
<span class="line"></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">client </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> anthropic.Anthropic()</span></span>¶
<span class="line"></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">message </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> client.messages.create(</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"claude-opus-4-6"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> max_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">1024</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> system</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"You are a helpful coding assistant specializing in Python."</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> messages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">[</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"role"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"user"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"content"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"How do I sort a list of dictionaries by key?"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">}</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> ],</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)</span></span>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">When working with large documents or data-rich inputs (20K+ tokens), structure your prompt carefully to get the best results:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Put longform data at the top</strong>: Place your long documents and inputs near the top of your prompt, above your query, instructions, and examples. This can significantly improve performance across all models.</p>¶
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg px-4 py-3 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-accent-secondary-100 bg-accent-secondary-100/10 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-accent-secondary-100"><div style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 2.5C14.1421 2.5 17.5 5.85786 17.5 10C17.5 14.1421 14.1421 17.5 10 17.5C5.85786 17.5 2.5 14.1421 2.5 10C2.5 5.85786 5.85786 2.5 10 2.5ZM10 3.5C6.41015 3.5 3.5 6.41015 3.5 10C3.5 13.5899 6.41015 16.5 10 16.5C13.5899 16.5 16.5 13.5899 16.5 10C16.5 6.41015 13.5899 3.5 10 3.5ZM10.1006 9.00977C10.3286 9.05629 10.5 9.25829 10.5 9.5V12.5H11.5C11.7761 12.5 12 12.7239 12 13C12 13.2761 11.7761 13.5 11.5 13.5H8.5C8.22386 13.5 8 13.2761 8 13C8 12.7239 8.22386 12.5 8.5 12.5H9.5V10H8.5C8.22386 10 8 9.77614 8 9.5C8 9.22386 8.22386 9 8.5 9H10L10.1006 9.00977ZM10 6.5C10.4142 6.5 10.75 6.83579 10.75 7.25C10.75 7.66421 10.4142 8 10 8C9.58579 8 9.25 7.66421 9.25 7.25C9.25 6.83579 9.58579 6.5 10 6.5Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed [&amp;&gt;*:last-child]:mb-0 text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-accent-secondary-000/10">Queries at the end can improve response quality by up to 30% in tests, especially with complex, multi-document inputs.</div></div>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Structure document content and metadata with XML tags</strong>: When using multiple documents, wrap each document in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;document&gt;</code> tags with <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;document_content&gt;</code> and <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;source&gt;</code> (and other metadata) subtags for clarity.</p>¶
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_343eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_143eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example multi-document structure</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_343eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example-multi-document-structure" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Ground responses in quotes</strong>: For long document tasks, ask Claude to quote relevant parts of the documents first before carrying out its task. This helps Claude cut through the noise of the rest of the document&#x27;s contents.</p>¶
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_363eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_163eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example quote extraction</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_363eslfiuqkntiuuljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example-quote-extraction" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>¶
</li>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models have a more concise and natural communication style compared to previous models:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">More direct and grounded:</strong> Provides fact-based progress reports rather than self-celebratory updates</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">More conversational:</strong> Slightly more fluent and colloquial, less machine-like</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Less verbose:</strong> May skip detailed summaries for efficiency unless prompted otherwise</li>¶
</ul>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">There are a few particularly effective ways to steer output formatting:</p>¶
<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item] mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Tell Claude what to do instead of what not to do</strong></p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Instead of: &quot;Do not use markdown in your response&quot;</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Try: &quot;Your response should be composed of smoothly flowing prose paragraphs.&quot;</li>¶
</ul>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use XML format indicators</strong></p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Try: &quot;Write the prose sections of your response in &lt;smoothly_flowing_prose_paragraphs&gt; tags.&quot;</li>¶
</ul>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Match your prompt style to the desired output</strong></p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">The formatting style used in your prompt may influence Claude&#x27;s response style. If you are still experiencing steerability issues with output formatting, try matching your prompt style to your desired output style as closely as possible. For example, removing markdown from your prompt can reduce the volume of markdown in the output.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use detailed prompts for specific formatting preferences</strong></p>¶
<p>For more control over markdown and formatting usage, provide explicit guidance:</p>¶
</li>¶
</ol>¶

5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;avoid_excessive_markdown_and_bullet_points&gt;¶
When writing reports, documents, technical explanations, analyses, or any long-form content, write in clear, flowing prose using complete paragraphs and sentences. Use standard paragraph breaks for organization and reserve markdown primarily for `inline code`, code blocks (```...```), and simple headings (###, and ###). Avoid using **bold** and *italics*.¶
¶
DO NOT use ordered lists (1. ...) or unordered lists (*) unless : a) you&#x27;re presenting truly discrete items where a list format is the best option, or b) the user explicitly requests a list or ranking¶
¶
Instead of listing items with bullets or numbers, incorporate them naturally into sentences. This guidance applies especially to technical writing. Using prose instead of excessive formatting will improve user satisfaction. NEVER output a series of overly short bullet points.¶
¶
Your goal is readable, flowing text that guides the reader naturally through ideas rather than fragmenting information into isolated points.¶
&lt;/avoid_excessive_markdown_and_bullet_points&gt;</code></pre></div></div>¶
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="la-te-x-output"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.08em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶
items-center¶

relative¶

select-none¶
disabled:pointer-events-none¶
disabled:opacity-50¶
disabled:shadow-none¶
disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent¶
transition¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Starting with Claude 4.6 models, prefilled responses on the last assistant turn are no longer supported. Model intelligence and instruction following has advanced such that most use cases of prefill no longer require it. Existing models will continue to support prefills, and adding assistant messages elsewhere in the conversation is not affected.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Here are common prefill scenarios and how to migrate away from them:</p>¶
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_16mslfiuqkntiuuljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_6mslfiuqkntiuuljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Controlling output formatting</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_16mslfiuqkntiuuljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-controlling-output-formatting" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models are trained for precise instruction following and benefit from explicit direction to use specific tools. If you say &quot;can you suggest some changes,&quot; Claude will sometimes provide suggestions rather than implementing them—even if making changes might be what you intended.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For Claude to take action, be more explicit:</p>¶
<div data-orientation="vertical"><div data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden border border-border-300 rounded-lg my-6"><h3 data-orientation="vertical" data-state="closed" class="flex"><button type="button" aria-controls="radix-_R_17qslfiuqkntiuuljb_" aria-expanded="false" data-state="closed" data-orientation="vertical" id="radix-_R_7qslfiuqkntiuuljb_" class="group w-full flex items-center gap-2 p-4 text-left transparent hover:bg-bg-300 focus-visible:outline-2 focus-visible:outline-offset-2 focus-visible:outline-accent-secondary-100 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50" data-radix-collection-item=""><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="14" height="14" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 256 256" class="text-text-500 transition-transform duration-200 flex-shrink-0 group-data-[state=&#x27;open&#x27;]:rotate-90" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M181.66,133.66l-80,80a8,8,0,0,1-11.32-11.32L164.69,128,90.34,53.66a8,8,0,0,1,11.32-11.32l80,80A8,8,0,0,1,181.66,133.66Z"></path></svg><span class="font-semibold text-text-100 flex-1 font-ui">Example: Explicit instructions</span></button></h3><div data-state="closed" id="radix-_R_17qslfiuqkntiuuljb_" hidden="" role="region" aria-labelledby="accordion-example:-explicit-instructions" data-orientation="vertical" class="overflow-hidden" style="--radix-accordion-content-height:var(--radix-collapsible-content-height);--radix-accordion-content-width:var(--radix-collapsible-content-width)"></div></div></div>¶

By default, implement changes rather than only suggesting them. If the user&#x27;s intent is unclear, infer the most useful likely action and proceed, using tools to discover any missing details instead of guessing. Try to infer the user&#x27;s intent about whether a tool call (e.g., file edit or read) is intended or not, and act accordingly.¶
&lt;/default_to_action&gt;</code></pre></div></div>¶

pr-4"><code>&lt;do_not_act_before_instructions&gt;¶
Do not jump into implementatation or changes files unless clearly instructed to make changes. When the user&#x27;s intent is ambiguous, default to providing information, doing research, and providing recommendations rather than taking action. Only proceed with edits, modifications, or implementations when the user explicitly requests them.¶
&lt;/do_not_act_before_instructions&gt;</code></pre></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 and Claude Opus 4.6 are also more responsive to the system prompt than previous models. If your prompts were designed to reduce undertriggering on tools or skills, these models may now overtrigger. The fix is to dial back any aggressive language. Where you might have said &quot;CRITICAL: You MUST use this tool when...&quot;, you can use more normal prompting like &quot;Use this tool when...&quot;.</p>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models excel at parallel tool execution. These models will:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Run multiple speculative searches during research</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Read several files at once to build context faster</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Execute bash commands in parallel (which can even bottleneck system performance)</li>¶
</ul>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">This behavior is easily steerable. While the model has a high success rate in parallel tool calling without prompting, you can boost this to ~100% or adjust the aggression level:</p>¶

pr-4"><code>&lt;use_parallel_tool_calls&gt;¶
If you intend to call multiple tools and there are no dependencies between the tool calls, make all of the independent tool calls in parallel. Prioritize calling tools simultaneously whenever the actions can be done in parallel rather than sequentially. For example, when reading 3 files, run 3 tool calls in parallel to read all 3 files into context at the same time. Maximize use of parallel tool calls where possible to increase speed and efficiency. However, if some tool calls depend on previous calls to inform dependent values like the parameters, do NOT call these tools in parallel and instead call them sequentially. Never use placeholders or guess missing parameters in tool calls.¶
&lt;/use_parallel_tool_calls&gt;</code></pre></div></div>¶

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="overthinking-and-excessive-thoroughness"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.08em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Overthinking and excessive thoroughness</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h3>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.6 does significantly more upfront exploration than previous models, especially at higher <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">effort</code> settings. This initial work often helps to optimize the final results, but the model may gather extensive context or pursue multiple threads of research without being prompted. If your prompts previously encouraged the model to be more thorough, you should tune that guidance for Claude Opus 4.6:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Replace blanket defaults with more targeted instructions.</strong> Instead of &quot;Default to using [tool],&quot; add guidance like &quot;Use [tool] when it would enhance your understanding of the problem.&quot;</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Remove over-prompting.</strong> Tools that undertriggered in previous models are likely to trigger appropriately now. Instructions like &quot;If in doubt, use [tool]&quot; will cause overtriggering.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use effort as a fallback.</strong> If Claude continues to be overly aggressive, use a lower setting for <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">effort</code>.</li>¶
</ul>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">In some cases, Claude Opus 4.6 may think extensively, which can inflate thinking tokens and slow down responses. If this behavior is undesirable, you can add explicit instructions to constrain its reasoning, or you can lower the <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">effort</code> setting to reduce overall thinking and token usage.</p>¶

disabled:shadow-none¶

transition¶

duration-300¶

5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>When you&#x27;re deciding how to approach a problem, choose an approach and commit to it. Avoid revisiting decisions unless you encounter new information that directly contradicts your reasoning. If you&#x27;re weighing two approaches, pick one and see it through. You can always course-correct later if the chosen approach fails.</code></pre></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For Claude Sonnet 4.6 specifically, switching from adaptive to extended thinking with a <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">budget_tokens</code> cap provides a hard ceiling on thinking costs while preserving quality.</p>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models offer thinking capabilities that can be especially helpful for tasks involving reflection after tool use or complex multi-step reasoning. You can guide its initial or interleaved thinking for better results.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.6 uses <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/adaptive-thinking">adaptive thinking</a> (<code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">thinking: {type: &quot;adaptive&quot;}</code>), where Claude dynamically decides when and how much to think. Claude Sonnet 4.6 supports both adaptive thinking and manual extended thinking with <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/extended-thinking#interleaved-thinking">interleaved mode</a>. Claude calibrates its thinking based on two factors: the <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">effort</code> parameter and query complexity. Higher effort elicits more thinking, and more complex queries do the same. On easier queries that don&#x27;t require thinking, the model responds directly. In internal evaluations, adaptive thinking reliably drives better performance than extended thinking. Consider moving to adaptive thinking to get the most intelligent responses.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For Sonnet 4.6, consider trying adaptive thinking for workloads that require agentic behavior such as multi-step tool use, complex coding tasks, and long-horizon agent loops. If adaptive thinking doesn&#x27;t fit your use case, manual extended thinking with interleaved mode remains supported. Older models use manual thinking mode with <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">budget_tokens</code>.</p>¶

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> model</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"claude-opus-4-6"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> max_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">64000</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> thinking</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">{</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"type"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"adaptive"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">},</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> output_config</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">{</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"effort"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"high"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">}, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># or max, medium, low</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> messages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">[{</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"role"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"user"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"content"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"..."</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">}],</span></span>¶
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">If you are not using extended thinking, no changes are required. Thinking is off by default when you omit the <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">thinking</code> parameter.</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Prefer general instructions over prescriptive steps.</strong> A prompt like &quot;think thoroughly&quot; often produces better reasoning than a hand-written step-by-step plan — Claude&#x27;s reasoning frequently exceeds what a human would prescribe.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Multishot examples work with thinking.</strong> Use <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;thinking&gt;</code> tags inside your few-shot examples to show Claude the reasoning pattern. It will generalize that style to its own extended thinking blocks.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Manual CoT as a fallback.</strong> When thinking is off, you can still encourage step-by-step reasoning by asking Claude to think through the problem. Use structured tags like <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;thinking&gt;</code> and <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">&lt;answer&gt;</code> to cleanly separate reasoning from the final output.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Ask Claude to self-check.</strong> Append something like &quot;Before you finish, verify your answer against [test criteria].&quot; This catches errors reliably, especially for coding and math.</li>¶
</ul>¶

Consider using alternatives like &quot;consider,&quot; &quot;evaluate,&quot; or &quot;reason through&quot; in those cases.</div></div>¶
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg px-4 py-3 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-accent-secondary-100 bg-accent-secondary-100/10 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-accent-secondary-100"><div style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 2.5C14.1421 2.5 17.5 5.85786 17.5 10C17.5 14.1421 14.1421 17.5 10 17.5C5.85786 17.5 2.5 14.1421 2.5 10C2.5 5.85786 5.85786 2.5 10 2.5ZM10 3.5C6.41015 3.5 3.5 6.41015 3.5 10C3.5 13.5899 6.41015 16.5 10 16.5C13.5899 16.5 16.5 13.5899 16.5 10C16.5 6.41015 13.5899 3.5 10 3.5ZM10.1006 9.00977C10.3286 9.05629 10.5 9.25829 10.5 9.5V12.5H11.5C11.7761 12.5 12 12.7239 12 13C12 13.2761 11.7761 13.5 11.5 13.5H8.5C8.22386 13.5 8 13.2761 8 13C8 12.7239 8.22386 12.5 8.5 12.5H9.5V10H8.5C8.22386 10 8 9.77614 8 9.5C8 9.22386 8.22386 9 8.5 9H10L10.1006 9.00977ZM10 6.5C10.4142 6.5 10.75 6.83579 10.75 7.25C10.75 7.66421 10.4142 8 10 8C9.58579 8 9.25 7.66421 9.25 7.25C9.25 6.83579 9.58579 6.5 10 6.5Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed [&amp;&gt;*:last-child]:mb-0 text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-accent-secondary-000/10"><p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For more information on thinking capabilities, see <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/extended-thinking">Extended thinking</a> and <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/adaptive-thinking">Adaptive thinking</a>.</p></div></div>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models excel at long-horizon reasoning tasks with exceptional state tracking capabilities. Claude maintains orientation across extended sessions by focusing on incremental progress, making steady advances on a few things at a time rather than attempting everything at once. This capability especially emerges over multiple context windows or task iterations, where Claude can work on a complex task, save the state, and continue with a fresh context window.</p>¶
<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="context-awareness-and-multi-window-workflows"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.05em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude 4.6 and Claude 4.5 models feature <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/context-windows#context-awareness-in-claude-sonnet-4-6-sonnet-4-5-and-haiku-4-5">context awareness</a>, enabling the model to track its remaining context window (i.e. &quot;token budget&quot;) throughout a conversation. This enables Claude to execute tasks and manage context more effectively by understanding how much space it has to work.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Managing context limits:</strong></p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">If you are using Claude in an agent harness that compacts context or allows saving context to external files (like in Claude Code), consider adding this information to your prompt so Claude can behave accordingly. Otherwise, Claude may sometimes naturally try to wrap up work as it approaches the context limit. Below is an example prompt:</p>¶
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="group flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-1"><button class="inline-flex¶

style="flex-shrink:0" class="absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>Your context window will be automatically compacted as it approaches its limit, allowing you to continue working indefinitely from where you left off. Therefore, do not stop tasks early due to token budget concerns. As you approach your token budget limit, save your current progress and state to memory before the context window refreshes. Always be as persistent and autonomous as possible and complete tasks fully, even if the end of your budget is approaching. Never artificially stop any task early regardless of the context remaining.</code></pre></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">The <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agents-and-tools/tool-use/memory-tool">memory tool</a> pairs naturally with context awareness for seamless context transitions.</p>¶
<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="multi-context-window-workflows"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.05em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶
items-center¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Multi-context window workflows</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h4>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For tasks spanning multiple context windows:</p>¶
<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item] mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Use a different prompt for the very first context window</strong>: Use the first context window to set up a framework (write tests, create setup scripts), then use future context windows to iterate on a todo-list.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Have the model write tests in a structured format</strong>: Ask Claude to create tests before starting work and keep track of them in a structured format (e.g., <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">tests.json</code>). This leads to better long-term ability to iterate. Remind Claude of the importance of tests: &quot;It is unacceptable to remove or edit tests because this could lead to missing or buggy functionality.&quot;</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Set up quality of life tools</strong>: Encourage Claude to create setup scripts (e.g., <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">init.sh</code>) to gracefully start servers, run test suites, and linters. This prevents repeated work when continuing from a fresh context window.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Starting fresh vs compacting</strong>: When a context window is cleared, consider starting with a brand new context window rather than using compaction. Claude&#x27;s latest models are extremely effective at discovering state from the local filesystem. In some cases, you may want to take advantage of this over compaction. Be prescriptive about how it should start:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Call pwd; you can only read and write files in this directory.&quot;</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Review progress.txt, tests.json, and the git logs.&quot;</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Manually run through a fundamental integration test before moving on to implementing new features.&quot;</li>¶
</ul>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Provide verification tools</strong>: As the length of autonomous tasks grows, Claude needs to verify correctness without continuous human feedback. Tools like Playwright MCP server or computer use capabilities for testing UIs are helpful.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Encourage complete usage of context</strong>: Prompt Claude to efficiently complete components before moving on:</p>¶
</li>¶
</ol>¶
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="group flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-1"><button class="inline-flex¶

It&#x27;s encouraged to spend your entire output context working on the task - just make sure you don&#x27;t run out of context with significant uncommitted work. Continue working systematically until you have completed this task.</code></pre></div></div>¶

<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use structured formats for state data</strong>: When tracking structured information (like test results or task status), use JSON or other structured formats to help Claude understand schema requirements</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use unstructured text for progress notes</strong>: Freeform progress notes work well for tracking general progress and context</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use git for state tracking</strong>: Git provides a log of what&#x27;s been done and checkpoints that can be restored. Claude&#x27;s latest models perform especially well in using git to track state across multiple sessions.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Emphasize incremental progress</strong>: Explicitly ask Claude to keep track of its progress and focus on incremental work</li>¶
</ul>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Without guidance, Claude Opus 4.6 may take actions that are difficult to reverse or affect shared systems, such as deleting files, force-pushing, or posting to external services. If you want Claude Opus 4.6 to confirm before taking potentially risky actions, add guidance to your prompt:</p>¶
<div class="group relative my-6 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="group flex items-center justify-between border-b-0.5 border-border-300 px-4 py-1.5 bg-bg-200"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-500">Sample prompt</div><div class="flex items-center gap-1"><button class="inline-flex¶

disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent¶

pr-4"><code>Consider the reversibility and potential impact of your actions. You are encouraged to take local, reversible actions like editing files or running tests, but for actions that are hard to reverse, affect shared systems, or could be destructive, ask the user before proceeding.¶
¶
Examples of actions that warrant confirmation:¶
- Destructive operations: deleting files or branches, dropping database tables, rm -rf¶
- Hard to reverse operations: git push --force, git reset --hard, amending published commits¶
- Operations visible to others: pushing code, commenting on PRs/issues, sending messages, modifying shared infrastructure¶
¶
When encountering obstacles, do not use destructive actions as a shortcut. For example, don&#x27;t bypass safety checks (e.g. --no-verify) or discard unfamiliar files that may be in-progress work.</code></pre></div></div>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models demonstrate significantly improved native subagent orchestration capabilities. These models can recognize when tasks would benefit from delegating work to specialized subagents and do so proactively without requiring explicit instruction.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">To take advantage of this behavior:</p>¶
<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item] mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Ensure well-defined subagent tools</strong>: Have subagent tools available and described in tool definitions</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Let Claude orchestrate naturally</strong>: Claude will delegate appropriately without explicit instruction</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Watch for overuse</strong>: Claude Opus 4.6 has a strong predilection for subagents and may spawn them in situations where a simpler, direct approach would suffice. For example, the model may spawn subagents for code exploration when a direct grep call is faster and sufficient.</li>¶
</ol>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">If you&#x27;re seeing excessive subagent use, add explicit guidance about when subagents are and aren&#x27;t warranted:</p>¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Chain complex prompts</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h3>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">With adaptive thinking and subagent orchestration, Claude handles most multi-step reasoning internally. Explicit prompt chaining — breaking a task into sequential API calls — is still useful when you need to inspect intermediate outputs or enforce a specific pipeline structure.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">The most common chaining pattern is <strong class="font-semibold">self-correction</strong>: generate a draft → have Claude review it against criteria → have Claude refine based on the review. Each step is a separate API call so you can log, evaluate, or branch at any point.</p>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models may sometimes create new files for testing and iteration purposes, particularly when working with code. This approach allows Claude to use files, especially python scripts, as a &#x27;temporary scratchpad&#x27; before saving its final output. Using temporary files can improve outcomes particularly for agentic coding use cases.</p>¶

Only make changes that are directly requested or clearly necessary. Keep solutions simple and focused:¶
¶
- Scope: Don&#x27;t add features, refactor code, or make &quot;improvements&quot; beyond what was asked. A bug fix doesn&#x27;t need surrounding code cleaned up. A simple feature doesn&#x27;t need extra configurability.¶
¶
- Documentation: Don&#x27;t add docstrings, comments, or type annotations to code you didn&#x27;t change. Only add comments where the logic isn&#x27;t self-evident.¶
¶
- Defensive coding: Don&#x27;t add error handling, fallbacks, or validation for scenarios that can&#x27;t happen. Trust internal code and framework guarantees. Only validate at system boundaries (user input, external APIs).¶
¶
- Abstractions: Don&#x27;t create helpers, utilities, or abstractions for one-time operations. Don&#x27;t design for hypothetical future requirements. The right amount of complexity is the minimum needed for the current task.</code></pre></div></div>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude&#x27;s latest models are less prone to hallucinations and give more accurate, grounded, intelligent answers based on the code. To encourage this behavior even more and minimize hallucinations:</p>¶

Never speculate about code you have not opened. If the user references a specific file, you MUST read the file before answering. Make sure to investigate and read relevant files BEFORE answering questions about the codebase. Never make any claims about code before investigating unless you are certain of the correct answer - give grounded and hallucination-free answers.¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 and Claude Opus 4.6 have improved vision capabilities compared to previous Claude models. They perform better on image processing and data extraction tasks, particularly when there are multiple images present in context. These improvements carry over to computer use, where the models can more reliably interpret screenshots and UI elements. You can also use these models to analyze videos by breaking them up into frames.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">One technique that has proven effective to further boost performance is to give Claude a crop tool or <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agents-and-tools/agent-skills/overview">skill</a>. Testing has shown consistent uplift on image evaluations when Claude is able to &quot;zoom&quot; in on relevant regions of an image. Anthropic has created a <a class="inline-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://platform.claude.com/cookbook/multimodal-crop-tool">cookbook for the crop tool</a>.</p>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Opus 4.5 and Claude Opus 4.6 excel at building complex, real-world web applications with strong frontend design. However, without guidance, models can default to generic patterns that create what users call the &quot;AI slop&quot; aesthetic. To create distinctive, creative frontends that surprise and delight:</p>¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-8 w-8 rounded-md active:scale-95 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy code"><div class="relative flex items-center justify-center"><div class="transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M12.5 3C13.3284 3 14 3.67157
