13H12.5C12.7761 13 13 12.7761 13 12.5V4.5C13 4.22386 12.7761 4 12.5 4H4.5Z"></path></svg></div><div class="absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="absolute transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 opacity-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M15.1883 5.10908C15.3699 4.96398 15.6346 4.96153 15.8202 5.11592C16.0056 5.27067 16.0504 5.53125 15.9403 5.73605L15.8836 5.82003L8.38354 14.8202C8.29361 14.9279 8.16242 14.9925 8.02221 14.9989C7.88203 15.0051 7.74545 14.9526 7.64622 14.8534L4.14617 11.3533L4.08172 11.2752C3.95384 11.0811 3.97542 10.817 4.14617 10.6463C4.31693 10.4755 4.58105 10.4539 4.77509 10.5818L4.85321 10.6463L7.96556 13.7586L15.1161 5.1794L15.1883 5.10908Z"></path></svg></div></div></button></div></div><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;frontend_aesthetics&gt;¶
You tend to converge toward generic, &quot;on distribution&quot; outputs. In frontend design, this creates what users call the &quot;AI slop&quot; aesthetic. Avoid this: make creative, distinctive frontends that surprise and delight.¶
¶
Focus on:¶
- Typography: Choose fonts that are beautiful, unique, and interesting. Avoid generic fonts like Arial and Inter; opt instead for distinctive choices that elevate the frontend&#x27;s aesthetics.¶
- Color &amp; Theme: Commit to a cohesive aesthetic. Use CSS variables for consistency. Dominant colors with sharp accents outperform timid, evenly-distributed palettes. Draw from IDE themes and cultural aesthetics for inspiration.¶
- Motion: Use animations for effects and micro-interactions. Prioritize CSS-only solutions for HTML. Use Motion library for React when available. Focus on high-impact moments: one well-orchestrated page load with staggered reveals (animation-delay) creates more delight than scattered micro-interactions.¶
- Backgrounds: Create atmosphere and depth rather than defaulting to solid colors. Layer CSS gradients, use geometric patterns, or add contextual effects that match the overall aesthetic.¶
¶
Avoid generic AI-generated aesthetics:¶
- Overused font families (Inter, Roboto, Arial, system fonts)¶
- Clichéd color schemes (particularly purple gradients on white backgrounds)¶
- Predictable layouts and component patterns¶
- Cookie-cutter design that lacks context-specific character¶
¶
Interpret creatively and make unexpected choices that feel genuinely designed for the context. Vary between light and dark themes, different fonts, different aesthetics. You still tend to converge on common choices (Space Grotesk, for example) across generations. Avoid this: it is critical that you think outside the box!¶
&lt;/frontend_aesthetics&gt;</code></pre></div></div>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">You can also refer to the <a class="inline-link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/blob/main/plugins/frontend-design/skills/frontend-design/SKILL.md">full skill definition</a>.</p>¶
<h2 class="font-heading leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="migration-considerations"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.175em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶
items-center¶
justify-center¶
relative¶
shrink-0¶
can-focus¶
select-none¶
disabled:pointer-events-none¶
disabled:opacity-50¶
disabled:shadow-none¶
disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent¶
transition¶
font-base¶
duration-300¶
ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Migration considerations</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h2>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">When migrating to Claude 4.6 models from earlier generations:</p>¶
<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item] mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Be specific about desired behavior</strong>: Consider describing exactly what you&#x27;d like to see in the output.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Frame your instructions with modifiers</strong>: Adding modifiers that encourage Claude to increase the quality and detail of its output can help better shape Claude&#x27;s performance. For example, instead of &quot;Create an analytics dashboard&quot;, use &quot;Create an analytics dashboard. Include as many relevant features and interactions as possible. Go beyond the basics to create a fully-featured implementation.&quot;</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Request specific features explicitly</strong>: Animations and interactive elements should be requested explicitly when desired.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Update thinking configuration</strong>: Claude 4.6 models use <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/adaptive-thinking">adaptive thinking</a> (<code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">thinking: {type: &quot;adaptive&quot;}</code>) instead of manual thinking with <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">budget_tokens</code>. Use the <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/effort">effort parameter</a> to control thinking depth.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Migrate away from prefilled responses</strong>: Prefilled responses on the last assistant turn are deprecated starting with Claude 4.6 models. See <a class="inline-link" href="#migrating-away-from-prefilled-responses">Migrating away from prefilled responses</a> for detailed guidance on alternatives.</p>¶
</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Tune anti-laziness prompting</strong>: If your prompts previously encouraged the model to be more thorough or use tools more aggressively, dial back that guidance. Claude 4.6 models are significantly more proactive and may overtrigger on instructions that were needed for previous models.</p>¶
</li>¶
</ol>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">For detailed migration steps, see the <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/about-claude/models/migration-guide">Migration guide</a>.</p>¶
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="migrating-from-claude-sonnet-4-5-to-claude-sonnet-4-6"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.08em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

disabled:shadow-none¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Migrating from Claude Sonnet 4.5 to Claude Sonnet 4.6</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h3>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Claude Sonnet 4.6 defaults to an effort level of <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">high</code>, in contrast to Claude Sonnet 4.5 which had no effort parameter. Consider adjusting the effort parameter as you migrate from Claude Sonnet 4.5 to Claude Sonnet 4.6. If not explicitly set, you may experience higher latency with the default effort level.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Recommended effort settings:</strong></p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Medium</strong> for most applications</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Low</strong> for high-volume or latency-sensitive workloads</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Set a large max output token budget (64k tokens recommended) at medium or high effort to give the model room to think and act</li>¶
</ul>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">When to use Opus 4.6 instead:</strong> For the hardest, longest-horizon problems (large-scale code migrations, deep research, extended autonomous work), Opus 4.6 remains the right choice. Sonnet 4.6 is optimized for workloads where fast turnaround and cost efficiency matter most.</p>¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">If you&#x27;re not using extended thinking on Claude Sonnet 4.5, you can continue without it on Claude Sonnet 4.6. You should explicitly set effort to the level appropriate for your use case. At <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">low</code> effort with thinking disabled, you can expect similar or better performance relative to Claude Sonnet 4.5 with no extended thinking.</p>¶

<h4 class="text-lg font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="group relative pt-6 pb-2" id="if-you-re-using-extended-thinking"><div class="absolute hidden lg:flex lg:items-center lg:-ml-8 top-[calc(1.5rem+0.05em)]"><button class="inline-flex¶

relative¶

can-focus¶
select-none¶

<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">If you&#x27;re using extended thinking on Claude Sonnet 4.5, it continues to be supported on Claude Sonnet 4.6 with no changes needed to your thinking configuration. Consider keeping a thinking budget around 16k tokens. In practice, most tasks don&#x27;t use that much, but it provides headroom for harder problems without risk of runaway token usage.</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">For coding use cases</strong> (agentic coding, tool-heavy workflows, code generation):</p>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">Start with <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">medium</code> effort. If you find latency is too high, consider reducing effort to <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">low</code>. If you need higher intelligence, consider increasing effort to <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">high</code> or migrating to Opus 4.6.</p>¶

ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="inline" style="width:20px;height:20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="flex-shrink:0" class="inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>When to try adaptive thinking</div><div class="absolute top-0 -right-6 hidden lg:flex"></div></div></h4>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">The extended thinking paths above use <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">budget_tokens</code> for predictable token usage. If your workload fits one of the following patterns, consider trying <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/build-with-claude/adaptive-thinking">adaptive thinking</a> instead:</p>¶
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 mb-4">¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Autonomous multi-step agents:</strong> coding agents that turn requirements into working software, data analysis pipelines, and bug finding where the model runs independently across many steps. Adaptive thinking lets the model calibrate its reasoning per step, staying on path over longer trajectories. For these workloads, start at <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">high</code> effort. If latency or token usage is a concern, scale down to <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">medium</code>.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Computer use agents:</strong> Claude Sonnet 4.6 achieved best-in-class accuracy on computer use evaluations using adaptive mode.</li>¶
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Bimodal workloads:</strong> a mix of easy and hard tasks where adaptive skips thinking on simple queries and reasons deeply on complex ones.</li>¶
</ul>¶
<p class="mb-2 last:mb-0">When using adaptive thinking, evaluate <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">medium</code> and <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">high</code> effort on your tasks. The right level depends on your workload&#x27;s tradeoff between quality, latency, and token usage.</p>¶
